{"name":"addParagraph","start":[206],"attrs":{"styleId":"Text_20_body"}},
{"name":"addText","start":[206,1],"text":"The configuration data of an extension can be reused when another version of this extension is installed. That is, the options page may show different values, although the user never changed the settings and in the xcu file of extension are other values."},

{"name":"addText","start":[213,1],"text":"The Same Extension Installed as Shared and User Extension"},
{"name":"addParagraph","start":[214],"attrs":{"styleId":"Text_20_body"}},
{"name":"addText","start":[214,1],"text":"If the same extension, or different versions of it, is installed as user and shared extension, then the Extension Manager shows only the options dialog for the user extension."},
{"name":"addParagraph","start":[215],"attrs":{"styleId":"Note"}},
{"name":"addText","start":[215,1],"text":"Reasoning: Provided that both extensions use the same configuration schema, then changes in the options dialog will be saved in the same configuration data. That is, changes made to the options of one extension overwrite the settings made in the options dialog of the other. If the configuration data contain URLs with %origin%, and the URL is expanded then it points into the directory of the user extension. This is important, when different versions are installed and the data referenced by the URL is different. When the values change in different versions of the extension, then the user may see inconsistent default values in the options dialog. For example, data item \u201cA\u201d has the value \u201ca\u201d and was installed by a shared extension. Now a newer version is installed as user extension and this extension defines that data item \u201cA\u201d has the value \u201cb\u201d. When one opened the options dialog for the shared extension then one would see value \u201cb\u201d instead of \u201ca\u201d, which was the case before the user extension was installed. After uninstalling the user extension the options dialog would again show value \u201ca\u201d. This behavior occurs only if the user has not yet modified \u201cA\u201d. Then the modified value would be shown in either case."},
{"name":"addParagraph","start":[216],"attrs":{"styleId":"Text_20_body"}},

{"name":"addParagraph","start":[300],"attrs":{"styleId":"Text_20_body"}},
{"name":"addText","start":[300,1],"text":"Currently the modified data remains in the user layer of the configuration even if the extension, including the xcu and xcs files is uninstalled. That is, the new version of the extension automatically uses the modified data unless it uses a different schema. It would be reasonable to allow to remove data in the user layer for data which has been defined by the extension. Then an extension could define in its description.xml if it want to reuse the data and could also specify the versions of the extensions from which it would reuse the data."},
{"name":"addParagraph","start":[301],"attrs":{"styleId":"Text_20_body"}},
{"name":"addText","start":[301,1],"text":"This would make it necessary to extract exactly the values which have been modified by the user. This happens before the extension is uninstalled. When the new version is installed then the previously extracted data is restored in the configuration. However, this is very difficult or maybe impossible to achieve with the current configuration, because it merges different layers to obtain one view on the data."},
{"name":"addParagraph","start":[302],"attrs":{"styleId":"Text_20_body"}},
